You can disable this feature in the settings page \"Synchronize map with compass (when follow or play is unactive)\". This way, if you go from point A to point B, you can record the route.\r\n\r\n3) Follow me and don't draw route on the map. In the menu you must click on \"Start follow me / Stop follow me\".
